              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",

              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",

              "        async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "          const element = document.querySelector('#df-7b2bdd06-b743-4eb7-8d34-855d7dba6724');\n",
              "          const dataTable =\n",
              "            await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                     [key], {});\n",
              "          if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "          const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",
              "    </div>\n",
              "  </div>\n",

              "    }\n",
              "\n",
              "    .colab-df-convert:hover {\n",
              "      background-color: #E2EBFA;\n",
              "      box-shadow: 0px 1px 2px rgba(60, 64, 67, 0.3), 0px 1px 3px 1px rgba(60, 64, 67, 0.15);\n",
              "      fill: #174EA6;\n",
              "    }\n",
              "\n",
              "    [theme=dark] .colab-df-convert {\n",
              "      background-color: #3B4455;\n",
              "      fill: #D2E3FC;\n",
              "    }\n",
              "\n",
              "    [theme=dark] .colab-df-convert:hover {\n",
              "      background-color: #434B5C;\n",
              "      box-shadow: 0px 1px 3px 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.15);\n",
              "      filter: drop-shadow(0px 1px 2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3));\n",
              "      fill: #FFFFFF;\n",
              "    }\n",
              "  </style>\n",
              "\n",
              "      <script>\n",
              "        const buttonEl =\n",
              "          document.querySelector('#df-ef550d9a-ee41-4562-88a7-1d4d90440450 button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "        buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "          google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "        async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "          const element = document.querySelector('#df-ef550d9a-ee41-4562-88a7-1d4d90440450');\n",
              "          const dataTable =\n",
              "            await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                     [key], {});\n",
              "          if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "          const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",
              "    </div>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "  "
            ]
          },
          "metadata": {},
          "execution_count": 23
        }

              "\n",
              "        async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "          const element = document.querySelector('#df-b1f83653-4132-4dff-a8ef-e52879de17c4');\n",
              "          const dataTable =\n",
              "            await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                     [key], {});\n",
              "          if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "          const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",
              "    </div>\n",

              "        }\n",

              "        const buttonEl =\n",
              "          document.querySelector('#df-10c36165-ded4-4cbf-a47c-6a0c9ecc6c80 button.colab-df-convert');\n",
              "        buttonEl.style.display =\n",
              "          google.colab.kernel.accessAllowed ? 'block' : 'none';\n",
              "\n",
              "        async function convertToInteractive(key) {\n",
              "          const element = document.querySelector('#df-10c36165-ded4-4cbf-a47c-6a0c9ecc6c80');\n",
              "          const dataTable =\n",
              "            await google.colab.kernel.invokeFunction('convertToInteractive',\n",
              "                                                     [key], {});\n",
              "          if (!dataTable) return;\n",
              "\n",
              "          const docLinkHtml = 'Like what you see? Visit the ' +\n",
              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",
              "    </div>\n",
              "  </div>\n",
              "  "
            ]

              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",
              "          await google.colab.output.renderOutput(dataTable, element);\n",
              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",

              "            '<a target=\"_blank\" href=https://colab.research.google.com/notebooks/data_table.ipynb>data table notebook</a>'\n",
              "            + ' to learn more about interactive tables.';\n",
              "          element.innerHTML = '';\n",
              "          dataTable['output_type'] = 'display_data';\n",

              "          const docLink = document.createElement('div');\n",
              "          docLink.innerHTML = docLinkHtml;\n",
              "          element.appendChild(docLink);\n",
              "        }\n",
              "      </script>\n",

        "    clf = cl\n",
        "    clf.fit(x_train, y_train)\n",
        "    accuracy = clf.score(x_test, y_test)*100\n",
        "    print('Accuracy of %r Classifier = %2f' % (cl, accuracy) + ' %')\n",
        "    print('\\n')"

      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\n",
        "sc=StandardScaler()\n",
        "x_train=sc.fit_transform(x_train)\n",
        "x_test=sc.transform(x_test)"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "C8xPAzoBcKdr"
      },
      "execution_count": null,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "execution_count": null,
      "metadata": {
        "id": "iaM4_XknpJFs"
      },
      "outputs": [],
      "source": [
        "                                                                                     # Start by creating class\n",
        "class NaiveBayes:\n",
        "    \n",
        "                                                                                     # fit methods trains the data\n",
        "    def fit(self,x,y):                                                               # here self is the variable which refers to current object of class \n",
        "        number_of_sample,number_of_features = x.shape                                # returns shape of X which is NxD dimensional\n",
        "                                                                                     # categories contains classes in Y uniquely due to Set\n",
        "        self.categories=np.unique(y)\n",
        "        \n",
        "                                                                                     # number_of_classes is the local variable\n",
        "        number_of_classes=len(self.categories)\n",
        "        \n",
        "                                                                                     # Initialising mean, var and priors\n",
        "        self._mean=np.zeros((number_of_classes,number_of_features),dtype=np.float64)\n",
        "        self._var=np.zeros((number_of_classes,number_of_features),dtype=np.float64)\n",
        "        self._prior=np.zeros((number_of_classes),dtype=np.float64)\n",
        "        \n",
        "                                                                                     # Calculating mean,var,prior based on categories in Y\n",
        "        for classes in self.categories:\n",
        "            x_classes=x[classes==y]                                                  # grouping into x_classes array according to category in y\n",
        "            self._mean[classes,:]=x_classes.mean(axis=0)                             # mean with each row of sample belonging particular column(features)\n",
        "            self._var[classes,:]=x_classes.var(axis=0)\n",
        "                                                                                     #number of sample in a class/ total samples\n",
        "            self._prior[classes]=(x_classes.shape[0]/float(number_of_sample)) \n",
        "          \n",
        "        \n",
        "            \n",
        "        \n",
        "        \n",
        "        \n",
        "    \n",
        "    \n",
        "                                                                                    # predict method make prediction\n",
        "    def predict(self,x):\n",
        "                                                                                    # posterior probablity dimension (number of sample,number of categories)\n",
        "        posteriorS=np.zeros((x.shape[0],len(self.categories)))\n",
        "        for classes in self.categories:                                             # calculating posterior with log of class_conditional probablity + log prior \n",
        "            posteriorS[:,classes]=mvn.logpdf(x,\n",
        "                                             mean=self._mean[classes,:],\n",
        "                                             cov=self._var[classes,:]) + self._prior[classes]\n",
        "        return np.argmax(posteriorS,axis=1)\n",
        "        \n",
        "    def accuracy(self,y_true,predicted):\n",
        "        return np.mean(y_true==predicted)"
      ]
    },

      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "# Predicting the labels for the test dataset\n",
        "y_pred = nb.predict(x_test)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Calculating true positives, false positives, false negatives, and true negatives\n",
        "TP = sum((y_test == 1) & (y_pred == 1))\n",
        "FP = sum((y_test == 0) & (y_pred == 1))\n",
        "FN = sum((y_test == 1) & (y_pred == 0))\n",
        "TN = sum((y_test == 0) & (y_pred == 0))\n",
        "\n",
        "# Calculating precision, recall, and F1 score\n",
        "precision = TP / (TP + FP)*100\n",
        "recall = TP / (TP + FN)*100\n",
        "f1_score = 2 * (precision * recall) / (precision + recall)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Printing the precision, recall, and F1 score values\n",
        "print('Precision:', precision)\n",
        "print('Recall:', recall)\n",
        "print('F1 Score:', f1_score)"
      ],

    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "class NaiveBayes:\n",
        "    def __init__(self, var_smoothing=1e-9):\n",
        "        self.var_smoothing = var_smoothing\n",
        "\n",
        "    def fit(self, X, y):\n",
        "        self.classes_ = np.unique(y)\n",
        "        self.theta_ = np.zeros((len(self.classes_), X.shape[1]))\n",
        "        self.sigma_ = np.zeros((len(self.classes_), X.shape[1]))\n",
        "        self.class_prior_ = np.zeros(len(self.classes_))\n",
        "        \n",
        "        for i, c in enumerate(self.classes_):\n",
        "            X_c = X[y == c]\n",
        "            self.theta_[i] = np.mean(X_c, axis=0)\n",
        "            self.sigma_[i] = np.var(X_c, axis=0)\n",
        "            self.class_prior_[i] = X_c.shape[0] / X.shape[0]\n",
        "        \n",
        "        return self\n",
        "\n",
        "    def predict(self, X):\n",
        "        y_pred = []\n",
        "        for x in X:\n",
        "            posterior = []\n",
        "            for i, c in enumerate(self.classes_):\n",
        "                likelihood = np.exp(-0.5 * np.sum(np.log(2. * np.pi * self.sigma_[i, :]))\n",
        "                                     - 0.5 * np.sum(((x - self.theta_[i, :]) ** 2) / (self.sigma_[i, :])),\n",
        "                                     axis=0)\n",
        "                prior = self.class_prior_[i]\n",
        "                posterior.append(likelihood * prior)\n",
        "            y_pred.append(self.classes_[np.argmax(posterior)])\n",
        "        return np.array(y_pred)\n",
        "\n",
        "    def score(self, X, y):\n",
        "        y_pred = self.predict(X)\n",
        "        return accuracy_score(y, y_pred)\n"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "F3_xOYvYXw5h"
      },
      "execution_count": null,
      "outputs": []
